< Review>
It took a lot longer than planned to write this review, but I felt it necessary.

I had always hated dealing with car dealerships until my experience at Niello Acura. I had been in an accident a week or so prior, and they ended up totaling my vehicle. Went to the Roseville Automall on my way back from the Sierra College Used Car deal. After having a couple of bad experiences at some dealerships there, specifically the sales people, I decided to go see what used cars Niello Acura had. I walked into the showroom and asked where their used cars would be, and was directed towards them. As I was walking out the door, I heard someone say "I'm following behind you in case you have any questions, but won't bug you." I thought "Yeah, right."

Well, that's exactly what Chris Knutson did, he stayed back and let me and a buddy look at the cars they had there. When I found any that I was interested in, he assisted with absolutely no pressure. After taking a test drive, I decided upon what I wanted to purchase, and as politley and respectfully as can be imagined, we started "The Dance."

At no point did I feel that Chris was being anything other then respectful, as he would say "Thank you for the offer, I will take this back to my manager." Long story short, we finally agreed upon the purchase price, and when Chris was done with the sales paperwork, he introduced me to Brian Bladow in Finance who handled the rest. The great service continued there, even to the point of working with me to wait for a check to clear from my insurance company for the totaled vehicle almost a week later. When I brought the check in, I was greeted by Chris saying that he noticed one of my mirrors had a blackening to it, and he had the replacement ready to be installed. I was in and out within 30min or so.

Although I bought a Lexus, and plan to buy another when I'm in the market, the customer service, compassion and care was top notch at this dealership, and I would go back to see what they have when I'm ready.</Review>

That seemed to not bother him at all and he spent the next hour with me walking me through the different models and options .  Chris was very informative, pleasant and never in a rush, but truly interested in making sure that I had all the information I needed to make the right choice.  From my website review I had decided on the ILX hybrid 2013 model.  Once I got to the dealership the decision became much more difficult.  I looked at the ILX model, the TSX, TL, ZDX (a snappy all while drive car that looked really cool), MDX (big SUV), RDX (smaller SUV).  We first test drove the TSX, it handled great and really reminded me of the performance and handling of a 3 series BMW.  Then we test drove the ILX hybrid.  I had driven a Prius before, but in comparison, the ILX handled a lot more like a normal car then a hybrid.  What amazed me about all of the models was the technology inside.I played around with the voice control system, which, as Chris explained to me, was the Acura preferred method of handling technology in the car.  With a couple of helpful tips from Chris, I was able to program my home address into the Navigation system for directions and that while negotiating taking an exit and merging with other traffic.  The voice control actually controls pretty much all of the different systems in the car like radio and climate control.  I had given up using the voice control system in my current car (a BMW) since it was always more cumbersome then just hitting the corresponding button.Looking at all of the different models made my decision not easier, but a lot harder.  I will have to take another trip to the dealership with the rest of the family and hope that they will weigh in and make the decision easier.< /review>

<user_id>106778310333403340622< /user_id><user_name>W. Craig Clark</user_name>< date>
1528528002365</date>
<rating>4< /rating>< text>
I've been to a fair number of fish hatcheries in my life. They all seem to have several things in common. Lots of fish, in long pools. And normally plenty of food to feed them. This one exceeds many others in the area that surrounds it. They have a great path and nature area that you can walk on to learn all sorts of information about the area around you. There is also a nice amphitheater type area where I assume they could have classes come and learn some things in an open classroom type setting. Parking is great by the trail head. Though from what I understand the main entrance road is currently under construction.</text>

<Date>1528953987691< /Date><Review>Finally a Tea Brick opened up around here! I was passing by the other day when I saw it had popped up under a soft opening and was waiting for the next opportunity to pay a visit.

If you've been to the original Tea brick, it has almost the same menu (with some noticable additions) and overall business structure.

I got a Nutella Snow Milk and a Durian smoothie. The snowmilk's blended ice could have been finer, but was overall flavorful and packed with pudding and nutella. THE DURIAN SMOOTHIE was B-O-M-B; I've had many durian smoothies that ranged from fresh fruit kinds to the artificial powder versions, and I can honestly say that I have one of the best ones here. If you're into that sort of thing.

Sad thing is that it doesn't have wifi yet, but other than that it's a cool spot to hang out and maybe play card or board games.<//Review>< user>
